Function Name:- dbHandler
Insert into rmx_registers (rmx_id,cs,address,data) VALUES ('1','0','0','0') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE data='0';

Function Name:- dbHandler

-------------------------------------------------------------
Function Name:- flushOldServices

Function Name:- flushOldServices
